<t>CREATE TABLE audit_logs (id INT PRIMARY KEY, event_time TIMESTAMP, user_id INT, event_description TEXT);

CREATE TABLE user_profiles (user_id INT PRIMARY KEY, full_name TEXT, email TEXT, phone_number TEXT);
